# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="3cc19-102">.NET Framework 中的已过时成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3cc19-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3cc19-103">本文列出了 .NET Framework 4.5 和更高版本中已过时的类型成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3cc19-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3cc19-104">类型成员由程序集分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3cc19-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3cc19-105">本文未列出过时类型的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3cc19-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3cc19-106">有关过时类型的列表，请参阅[过时类型](obsolete-types.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3cc19-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="mscorlibdll"></a><span data-ttu-id="3cc19-107">mscorlib.dll</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3cc19-107">mscorlib.dll</span></span>
